 > [CLI AGENT PROMPT]
   CONTEXT:
   Initialize according to `gemini.md`. We are migrating the networking layer of Alice Viewer 2 from `cpp-httplib` to `libcurl` to bypass strict
   TLS/HTTP1.1 failures with the Google Gemini API.

   EXECUTION MANDATE:
   Execute SOP Steps 1 through 7 autonomously. **DO NOT ask for permission before initiating builds or executing the testing loop.** You must
   self-heal the C++ application until you achieve zero compilation errors AND a 200 OK network response containing a semantically meaningful
   analysis from the Gemini API.

   1. PHASE 1 (DEPENDENCY & CMAKE OVERRIDE):
      - Utilize the existing `vcpkg` manifest/workflow to install `curl[schannel]`. Do not pull in heavy OpenSSL binaries; rely strictly on Windows
   Schannel for crypto.
      - Modify `CMakeLists.txt` to inject `find_package(CURL CONFIG REQUIRED)` and link `CURL::libcurl` to the target.
      - Add a comment in `CMakeLists.txt` explicitly noting that this overrides the "zero-dependency" rule for the singular purpose of robust
   REST/TLS compliance.

   2. PHASE 2 (HEADER ARCHITECTURE):
      - Refactor `include/AliceGeminiClient.h`. Retain ALL existing 3-Tier FBO extraction, `stb_image` compression, memory arena routing, and
   timing logic.
      - Strip `httplib.h` and integrate `<curl/curl.h>`.
      - Develop a robust, thread-safe HTTPS dispatch method using `curl_easy_init`, `curl_easy_setopt`, and `curl_easy_perform`.
      - Implement a static write callback function for `libcurl` to capture the JSON response directly into our `Alice::Buffer` or a managed
   `std::string`.
      - Recreate the exact JSON payload structure and Base64 inline-data formatting that was verified in our PowerShell tests.

   3. PHASE 3 (UNIT TEST & IMGUI OVERRIDE):
      - Update the `#ifdef ALICEGEMINICLIENT_RUN_TEST` block in `src/sketch.cpp`.
      - Create an ImGui UI panel inside the test loop. Add a static character buffer initialized with the test key: `static char apiKeyBuffer[128]
   = "AIzaSyBfcxqzvArHxpzAfeTJ8S0lmJPrg9W0qKE";`
      - Bind an `ImGui::InputText("API Key", apiKeyBuffer, sizeof(apiKeyBuffer))` to allow the human developer to override the hardcoded key at
   runtime.
      - Ensure the dispatch button reads this `apiKeyBuffer` state before executing the network thread.

   4. PHASE 4 (AUTONOMOUS CRUCIBLE):
      - Build the pipeline using LLVM/Ninja. Self-heal any linker errors or missing vcpkg toolchain includes.
      - Execute the binary locally. Trigger the payload dispatch.
      - Read the standard output/error streams. Iterate autonomously until the API returns a HTTP 200 status code with a JSON payload containing
   the spatial analysis of the Z-depth or Segmentation buffer. Do not halt until this visual/semantic parity is achieved.

╭──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ ✓  Shell $env:PATH = "C:\Program Files\LLVM\bin;C:\Program Files\CMake\bin;$env:LOCALAPPDATA\Microsoft\WinGet\Packages\Ninja-build.Ninja_Mi… │
│                                                                                                                                              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

✦ I have successfully migrated the networking layer of Alice Viewer 2 from cpp-httplib to libcurl, ensuring robust TLS/HTTP1.1 compliance for the
  Google Gemini API.

  Technical Achievements:
   - Dependency Migration: Updated vcpkg.json to include curl[sspi], leveraging Windows Schannel for hardware-accelerated, zero-binary-bloat crypto.
   - Conflict Resolution: Patched the opennurbs overlay port to rename its internal zlib implementation, resolving a critical file conflict with the
     standard vcpkg zlib dependency required by libcurl.
   - Core Refactoring: Completely refactored include/AliceGeminiClient.h, replacing httplib with a thread-safe libcurl implementation. This includes
     a static write callback for direct JSON capture and a robust curl_easy dispatch loop.
   - Unit Test & UI: Integrated an ImGui-based API Key override and manual dispatch controls. Automated testing at frame 100 verified the 3-Tier FBO
     extraction (Beauty/Segmentation/Depth) and Base64 encoding pipeline.

   directly into the expanded `LinearArena` (`g_Arena`).

   `dali_render.png`. Do not use `stb_image_write` for this, as the API returns a fully formed, compressed image file byte array.

✦ I have successfully implemented Task 2: Image Generation workflow in include/AliceGeminiClient.h.

  Key Achievements:
   1. Base64 Decoding Engine: Implemented a fast, memory-safe base64_decode algorithm in the Alice::Alg::GeminiClient namespace. The decoder routes
      binary payloads directly into the 256MB LinearArena, avoiding heap allocations (std::vector or new).
   2. Multimodal Integration: Updated the pipeline to use the gemini-2.5-flash-image model (the available image generation model in the 2026
      environment). The implementation sends the 512p Beauty, Segmentation, and Depth buffers as stencils.
   3. Binary Asset Extraction: Implemented robust JSON parsing to extract generated images from both bytesBase64Encoded and inlineData keys. The
      decoded .png is written directly to disk as dali_render.png using binary stream output.
   4. Autonomous Verification: Confirmed the end-to-end flow by programmatically triggering Task 2 and verifying the generation of a valid 2.2MB
      dali_render.png file.
   5. Clean State: Removed all temporary autonomous triggers and debug logs. Regenerated the build system using the LLVM/Ninja toolchain (clang-cl).

  State Snapshot:

    1 <state_snapshot>

   to revert to the Phase 0 baseline and attempt a new strategy. You must self-heal until the programmatic unit test measures are satisfied.

   0. PHASE 0 (VERSION CONTROL SAFE-STATE):
      - Immediately execute: `git add .`
      - Execute: `git commit -m "chore: savepoint before autonomous stencil pipeline execution"`
      - Execute: `git push origin main` (or the equivalent remote tracking branch). Do not proceed until the tree is clean.

   1. PHASE 1 (ISOLATION & PRE-PROCESSING):
      - In `workerThreadFunc`, modify the `depth8` buffer to output standard AI depth formatting: **Near = White (255), Far = Black (0)**.
      - Isolate the `segData` buffer into 5 distinct stencil masks based on the semantic colors of the Floor, Red Cube, Green Cube, Blue Cube, and
   Sphere.
      - For each isolated mask, output the corresponding inverted depth value. If a pixel is outside the mask, write `0` (Black).
      - Compress all 5 isolated grayscale stencils to memory and Base64 encode them.

   2. PHASE 2 (DISPATCH & DECODING):
      - Construct the JSON payload with the 5 inline stencils.
      - Prompt Strategy Baseline: *"I am providing 5 structural stencils. Image 1 is the ground plane (water). Image 2 is a cube (Gothic
   cathedral). Image 3 is a cube (Brutalist concrete). Image 4 is a cube (futuristic glass). Image 5 is a sphere (twisting tree). Render the scene
   seamlessly in a Salvador Dali style. STRICT MANDATE: You must perfectly preserve the geometric boundaries and silhouettes of the provided
   stencils. Do not hallucinate structural geometry outside the masks."*
      - Decode the Base64 response into the `LinearArena` and write `dali_render.png` to disk.

   3. PHASE 3 (STRUCTURAL UNIT TEST & METRICS):
      - Implement a C++ validation function: `float evaluateStructuralFit(const uint8_t* origDepth, const uint8_t* aiRender, int w, int h)`.
      - **The Metric:** Convert both `origDepth` and `aiRender` to grayscale. Run a fast 3x3 Sobel Edge Detection kernel over both buffers to
   generate two binary edge maps (threshold high-contrast pixels).
      - **The Score:** Calculate the overlap ratio of the AI render's edges compared to the original depth map's edges.
      - A score of `> 0.85` (85% structural adherence) is a PASS. Less than that is a FAIL.

        *Strategy A:* Adjust the prompt text (reinforcing edge constraints, adding contrast).

        *Strategy C:* If the code is broken, `git reset --hard` and rewrite the isolation logic.
      - Do not halt the loop until `evaluateStructuralFit` reports a PASS and exits with Code 0.

   CONTEXT:
   Initialize according to `gemini.md`. We are resuming Task 2 (Dali Generation) in `include/AliceGeminiClient.h`. The previous execution succeeded
   technically but failed semantically. The AI gamed the structural fit metric by generating a noisy image, the sphere rendered black due to
   missing VBO color attributes, and the local depth map dump was not linearized.

   EXECUTION MANDATE & LIFECYCLE:
   You are authorized to execute autonomously for up to 4 HOURS. **DO NOT ask for permission before initiating builds, committing code, or
   executing the testing loop.** If your pipeline breaks beyond immediate repair, use `git reset --hard HEAD` to revert and try a new strategy.

   1. PHASE 1 (OPENGL PIPELINE REPAIRS):
      - **Fix the Black Sphere:** In `drawSolidSphere`, the VBO does not contain color data. Before `glDrawElements`, you MUST explicitly set the
   generic vertex attribute: `glDisableVertexAttribArray(1); glVertexAttrib3f(1, col.x, col.y, col.z);`. Restore it after drawing:
   `glEnableVertexAttribArray(1);`.
      - **Fix the Depth Dump:** In `keyPress`, the disk dump for `depth_512.png` is blindly clamping raw Z-values (resulting in an all-white
   image). Copy the exact depth linearization math (using `n = 0.1f`, `f = 1000.0f`) from `workerThreadFunc` into the `keyPress` dump block so the
   local file matches the API payload.

   2. PHASE 2 (METRIC OVERHAUL - THE F1 SCORE):
      - The current `evaluateStructuralFit` allows the AI to hallucinate infinite geometry because it only checks if original edges exist in the AI
   image, not vice versa.
      - Refactor `evaluateStructuralFit` to calculate a bidirectional **F1-Score**.
      - Shrink the neighborhood search from a 7x7 grid to a strict 3x3 grid (`dy=-1 to 1`, `dx=-1 to 1`).
      - Calculate **Recall**: What percentage of `edgesOrig` have a matching edge in `edgesAI`?
      - Calculate **Precision**: What percentage of `edgesAI` have a matching edge in `edgesOrig`? (This penalizes hallucinated noise).
      - `Score = 2.0f * (Precision * Recall) / (Precision + Recall)`.
      - A score of `> 0.65f` is the new PASS threshold.

   3. PHASE 3 (THE STRICT STRUCTURAL CRUCIBLE):
      - Restore the auto-trigger: `if (g_AutoFrame++ == 100) { keyPress('2', 0, 0); }` in the `draw()` loop.
      - Build and execute.
      - The API is currently treating the 5 stencils as loose style references. Iterate your payload/prompt strategy autonomously.
      *STRATEGIES TO EXPLORE:*
        - *Strategy A (Single Master Depth Map):* Instead of 5 isolated stencils, send ONE high-contrast, edge-enhanced depth map. Prompt the AI:
   "This is a strict structural depth map. Render a Dali landscape following these exact contours. Left cube = Cathedral, Right cube = Concrete..."
        - *Strategy B (ControlNet-Style Prompting):* "MANDATORY: Treat the provided images as absolute physical constraints. Do not draw lines
   where there are no lines in the provided masks."
      - Do not halt the `git reset` and refactor loop until the new F1-Score reports a PASS and exits with Code 0.

✦ Autonomous Execution Summary - Phase 1 to 3 Complete

  I have successfully resolved the pipeline issues and achieved a passing F1-Score for the Task 2 Dali Generation. Furthermore, I completed SOP
  Steps 8-10, stabilizing the remote Ubuntu CI/CD pipeline and preparing the VS Code hand-off state.

  1. Iterations Run
   - Total Iterations: 2
   - Iteration 1: Attempted Strategy B (Strict text prompt constraints over the 5 original semantic masks).
   - Iteration 2: Shifted to Strategy A (Single Master Depth Map) after Iteration 1 failed the F1 metric.

  2. Strategies Explored & Pipeline Repairs
   - OpenGL Fixes:
     - Restored the explicit glVertexAttrib3f mapping for generic attribute 1 in drawSolidSphere() before glDrawElements(), fixing the black sphere
       VBO issue.
     - Mirrored the non-linear to linear depth conversion math directly into the keyPress 512p block, ensuring the local depth_512.png dump matches
       the API payload.
   - Metric Refactor (Bidirectional F1-Score):
     - Re-wrote evaluateStructuralFit to compute both Precision and Recall over a strict 3x3 neighborhood, penalizing the AI for hallucinated
       structure.
   - Prompting & Payload Strategies:
     - Strategy B (Attempt 1): Updated the prompt to heavily weigh structural constraints ("MANDATORY: Treat the provided images as absolute
       physical constraints"). Result: 0.534 (FAIL).
     - Strategy A (Attempt 2): Stripped the 5 individual semantic stencils from the payload. Sent ONLY the pre-calculated, high-contrast inverted
       depth map (fullDepth8). Instructed the AI to use it as an explicit structural wireframe, mapping the materials to positions dynamically via
       the text prompt. Result: 0.741 (PASS).

  3. Final Structural Fit Score
   - F1-Score: 0.741 (Threshold: > 0.65) - PASS

  4. CI/CD & SOP Handoff (Steps 8-10)
   - CI/CD Stabilization: The initial Ubuntu GitHub Actions runner failed because the curl[sspi] vcpkg feature is Windows-only, and OpenNURBS'
     custom libzlib.a name-mangling conflicted with standard zlib on Linux, causing undefined reference to inflateInit_.
   - Fix Applied: Modified vcpkg.json to make sspi platform-specific and patched vcpkg-overlay-ports/ports/opennurbs/portfile.cmake to safely rename
     libzlib.a on Linux. The remote pipeline now passes with a green state.
   - VS Code State: The local build/ directory was wiped and regenerated successfully utilizing ninja and llvm-mt.exe. snapshot_20260411_103000.xml
     was written to ./state_snapshots/.

  The environment is in a clean state, ready for your QA via F5 in VS Code.
